## 3. Samuccayakkhandhakaṃ

3.The Chapter on Accumulation

### 1. Sukkavissaṭṭhi ^1

> [!TIP]- Links to [[cv13-brahmali-pali#^1|Brahmali Version]] and BMC2 
> [[bmc2#^ch19|BMC Chapter 19]] and the following cites:
>  
> ```query
> "VIN-CV13.1" file:bmc2 -queryblock
> ```


1.Emission of Semen

97. Tena samayena buddho bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā udāyī ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpanno hoti sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato [te bhikkhū bhagavato (syā.)] etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbaṃ –

97.At that time the Blessed One was dwelling at Sāvatthī, in Jeta Grove, Anāthapiṇḍika’s Monastery. Now at that time Venerable Udāyī had incurred one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. He informed the bhikkhus: “Venerables, I have incurred one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. How should I proceed?” They reported the matter to the Blessed One. “Then, bhikkhus, the Saṅgha should impose a six-night mānatta on the bhikkhu Udāyī for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. And it should be imposed thus:

Appaṭicchannamānattaṃ

The Unconcealed Mānatta

98. ‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā añjaliṃ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmi. Ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Dutiyampi, sohaṃ [dutiyampi (sī. ka.)] bhante, saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmi. Ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Tatiyampi sohaṃ [tatiyampi (sī. ka.)], bhante, saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmī’ti. ‘‘Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

98.“Then, bhikkhus, the bhikkhu Udāyī should approach the Saṅgha, arrange his upper robe over one shoulder, pay homage at the feet of the senior bhikkhus, sit in a squatting position, raise his joined palms, and should say thus: ‘Venerable sirs, I have incurred one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. Therefore, venerable sirs, I ask the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. Venerable sirs, I have incurred one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. For the second time, venerable sirs, I ask the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. Venerable sirs, I have incurred one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. For the third time, venerable sirs, I ask the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed.’ A competent and able bhikkhu should then inform the Saṅgha:

99. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

99.“Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This bhikkhu Udāyī has incurred one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. He asks the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. If it is agreeable to the Saṅgha, the Saṅgha may grant a six-night mānatta to the bhikkhu Udāyī for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. This is the motion.

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

“Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This bhikkhu Udāyī has incurred one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. He asks the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. The Saṅgha grants the bhikkhu Udāyī a six-night mānatta for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. Any venerable one who approves of granting a six-night mānatta to the bhikkhu Udāyī for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed, should remain silent. Any who disapproves should speak.”

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi – suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

“Venerable sirs, I speak on this matter a second time: may the Saṅgha hear me. This bhikkhu Udāyī has incurred one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. He asks the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. The Saṅgha grants the bhikkhu Udāyī a six-night mānatta for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. Any venerable one who approves of granting a six-night mānatta to the bhikkhu Udāyī for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed, should remain silent. Any who disapproves should speak.”

‘‘Tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi – suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

“Venerable sirs, I speak on this matter a third time: may the Saṅgha hear me. This bhikkhu Udāyī has incurred one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. He asks the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. The Saṅgha grants the bhikkhu Udāyī a six-night mānatta for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. Any venerable one who approves of granting a six-night mānatta to the bhikkhu Udāyī for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed, should remain silent. Any who disapproves should speak.”

‘‘Dinnaṃ saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

“A six-night mānatta has been granted by the Saṅgha to the bhikkhu Udāyī for one offense involving intentional emission of semen, which was unconcealed. The Saṅgha approves of it, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.”

Appaṭicchannaabbhānaṃ

Reinstatement of the Unconfessed

100. So ciṇṇamānatto bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbhetu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, abbhetabbo –

100.The monk who had completed the mānatta informed the monks: “Friends, I committed one offense—intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. I requested the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. The Saṅgha granted me a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. I have completed the mānatta. What should I do now?” They reported the matter to the Blessed One. “Well then, monks, let the Saṅgha reinstate the monk Udāyī. And, monks, he should be reinstated like this:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā añjaliṃ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo – ‘‘ahaṃ bhante ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ, sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ, bhante, ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmi.

Then, monks, the monk Udāyī should approach the Saṅgha, arrange his upper robe over one shoulder, pay homage at the feet of the senior monks, kneel down, raise his joined palms, and say thus: ‘Venerable sirs, I have committed an offense—intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. I requested the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. The Saṅgha granted me a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. Venerable sirs, having completed the mānatta, I now request the Saṅgha for reinstatement.’

‘‘Ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto dutiyampi, bhante, saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmi.

“Venerable sir, I committed one offense: intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. I requested the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. The Saṅgha granted me a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. Having completed the mānatta, I now, venerable sir, request the Saṅgha for reinstatement for a second time.”

‘‘Ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto tatiyampi, bhante, saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmīti. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

“Venerable sir, I committed one offense: an intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. I requested the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. The Saṅgha granted me a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. Having completed the mānatta, venerable sir, I now request the Saṅgha for reinstatement for the third time.” A competent and able monk should inform the Saṅgha:

101. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheyya. Esā ñatti.

101.“Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense: intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. He requests the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. The Saṅgha has granted a six-night mānatta to the monk Udāyī for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. Having completed the mānatta, he now requests the Saṅgha for reinstatement. If it is agreeable to the Saṅgha, the Saṅgha may reinstate the monk Udāyī. This is the motion.”

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

“Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense—intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. He has requested the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. The Saṅgha has granted a six-night mānatta to the monk Udāyī for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. Having completed the mānatta, he now requests reinstatement from the Saṅgha. The Saṅgha is reinstating the monk Udāyī. Let any venerable one who approves of the reinstatement of the monk Udāyī remain silent; let anyone who does not approve speak.”

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi – suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

“For the second time, I speak on this matter—venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense: intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. He has requested the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. The Saṅgha has granted a six-night mānatta to the monk Udāyī for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. Having completed the mānatta, he requests reinstatement from the Saṅgha. The Saṅgha reinstates the monk Udāyī. Venerable ones, whoever is in favor of the reinstatement of the monk Udāyī, let them remain silent; whoever is not in favor, let them speak.”

‘‘Tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi – suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

“For the third time, I speak on this matter—venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This monk Udāyī committed one offense: intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. He requested the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. The Saṅgha granted a six-night mānatta to the monk Udāyī for that one intentional emission of semen, unconfessed. Having completed the mānatta, he now requests reinstatement from the Saṅgha. The Saṅgha reinstates the monk Udāyī. If any venerable one approves of Udāyī’s reinstatement, let them remain silent; if any disapprove, let them speak.”

‘‘Abbhito saṅghena udāyī bhikkhu. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

“The monk Udāyī has been reinstated by the Saṅgha. The Saṅgha approves, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.”

Ekāhappaṭicchannaparivāsaṃ

A one-day concealed period of probation

102. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā udāyī ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpanno hoti sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo –

102.At that time, the Venerable Udāyī had committed one offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. He informed the monks: “Friends, I have committed one offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. How should I proceed?” They reported the matter to the Blessed One. “Well then, monks, let the Saṅgha grant the monk Udāyī a one-day period of probation for that one offense, an intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. And thus, monks, it should be granted:

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā añjaliṃ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbo. Tatiyampi yācitabbo. ‘‘Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

“Monks, the monk Udāyin should approach the Saṅgha, arrange his upper robe over one shoulder, pay homage at the feet of the senior monks, sit in a squatting position, raise his joined palms, and say: ‘Venerables, I have committed one offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. I request the Saṅgha for a one-day period of probation for this offense.’ He should be requested a second time. He should be requested a third time. A competent and capable monk should then inform the Saṅgha:

103. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

103.“Venerable Saṅgha, may the Saṅgha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense, a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. He asks the Saṅgha for a one-day period of probation for one offense, a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. If it seems right to the Saṅgha, the Saṅgha may grant Udāyī a one-day period of probation for one offense, a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. This is the motion.”

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

“Venerable Saṅgha, may the Saṅgha listen to me. This monk Udāyī has committed an offense entailing intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. He asks the Saṅgha for a one-day period of probation for this offense entailing intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. The Saṅgha grants the monk Udāyī a one-day period of probation for this offense entailing intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. Any venerable one who approves of granting a one-day period of probation to the monk Udāyī for this offense entailing intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day, let him be silent; anyone who disapproves, let him speak.”

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

“For the second time, I say this matter… For the third time, I say this matter….

‘‘Dinno saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāso. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

“The Saṅgha has granted a one-day period of probation to the monk Udāyī for one offense, a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. The Saṅgha approves, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.”

Ekāhappaṭicchannamānattaṃ

Mānatta for an Offense Concealed for One Day

104. So parivutthaparivāso bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbaṃ –

104.Having lived out his probation, that bhikkhu informed the bhikkhus: "Friends, I committed an offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. I requested the Sangha for one day of probation for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. The Sangha granted me one day of probation for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. Now that I have lived out my probation, how should I proceed?" They reported this matter to the Blessed One. "In that case, bhikkhus, let the Sangha grant the bhikkhu Udāyī six nights of mānatta for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. And this is how it should be done:

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ, bhante, parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ [yācitabbo (sī. evamuparipi)]. Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ [yācitabbo (sī. evamuparipi)]. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

"In that case, bhikkhus, the bhikkhu Udāyī should approach the Sangha... and should be addressed thus: 'Venerable sirs, I committed an offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. I requested the Sangha for one day of probation for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. The Sangha granted me one day of probation for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. Venerable sirs, having lived out my probation, I now request the Sangha for six nights of mānatta for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day.' He should make the request a second time. He should make the request a third time. A competent and capable bhikkhu should then inform the Sangha:

105. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

105."Venerable sirs, let the Sangha hear me. This bhikkhu Udāyī has committed an offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. He requested the Sangha for one day of probation for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. The Sangha granted the bhikkhu Udāyī one day of probation for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. Having lived out his probation, he now requests the Sangha for six nights of mānatta for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. If it seems fit to the Sangha, let the Sangha grant the bhikkhu Udāyī six nights of mānatta for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. This is the motion."

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

"Venerable sirs, let the Sangha hear me. This bhikkhu Udāyī has committed an offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. He requested the Sangha for one day of probation for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. The Sangha granted the bhikkhu Udāyī one day of probation for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. Having lived out his probation, he now requests the Sangha for six nights of mānatta for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. The Sangha grants the bhikkhu Udāyī six nights of mānatta for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. If the granting of six nights of mānatta for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day to the bhikkhu Udāyī is acceptable to any venerable one, let him be silent; if not, let him speak."

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

"For a second time I speak on this matter... For a third time I speak on this matter..."

‘‘Dinnaṃ saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

"The Sangha has granted the bhikkhu Udāyī six nights of mānatta for that offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for one day. The Sangha is agreeable, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it."

Ekāhappaṭicchannaabbhānaṃ

Reinstatement for a Single Day's Concealment

106. So ciṇṇamānatto bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbhetu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, abbhetabbo –

106.Having completed the period of discipline, he informed the monks: "Friends, I committed one offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. I requested the Saṅgha for a one-day probationary period for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. The Saṅgha granted me a one-day probationary period for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. Having completed the probationary period, I requested the Saṅgha for a six-night period of discipline for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. The Saṅgha granted me a six-night period of discipline for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. I have completed the period of discipline. What should I do now?" They reported the matter to the Blessed One. "Well then, monks, let the Saṅgha reinstate the monk Udāyī. And monks, he should be reinstated like this—"

‘‘Tena bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ, bhante, ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

Then, monks, that monk Udāyī should approach the Saṅgha … and say thus: ‘Venerable sirs, I committed one offense: a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. For that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day, I requested the Saṅgha for a one-day probationary period. The Saṅgha granted me a one-day probationary period for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. Having completed the probationary period, I requested the Saṅgha for a six-night period of discipline for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. The Saṅgha granted me a six-night period of discipline for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. Venerable sirs, having completed the period of discipline, I request the Saṅgha for reinstatement.’ It should be requested a second time. It should be requested a third time. A competent and capable monk should inform the Saṅgha:

107. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheyya. Esā ñatti.

107.Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This monk Udāyin has committed one offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. He requested the Saṅgha for a one-day probationary period for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyin a one-day probationary period for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. Having completed the probationary period, he requested the Saṅgha for a six-night period of discipline for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyin a six-night period of discipline for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. Having completed the period of discipline, he requests the Saṅgha for reinstatement. If the Saṅgha is ready, let the Saṅgha reinstate the monk Udāyin. This is the motion.

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This monk Udāyin has committed one offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. He requested the Saṅgha for a one-day probationary period for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyin a one-day probationary period for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. Having completed the probationary period, he requested the Saṅgha for a six-night period of discipline for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyin a six-night period of discipline for that one offense of deliberate emission of semen, concealed for one day. Having completed the period of discipline, he asks the Saṅgha for reinstatement. The Saṅgha reinstates the monk Udāyin. Let any venerable one who approves of the reinstatement of the monk Udāyin remain silent; let anyone who disapproves speak.

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

For the second time, I say this… For the third time, I say this…

‘‘Abbhito saṅghena udāyī bhikkhu. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

The monk Udāyin has been reinstated by the Saṅgha. The Saṅgha approves; therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.

Pañcāhappaṭicchannaparivāso

Probation for an offense concealed for five days.

108. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā udāyī ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpanno hoti sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ dvīhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… tīhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… catūhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo –

108.At that time, Venerable Udāyī had committed an offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for two days… concealed for three days… concealed for four days… concealed for five days. He informed the monks: “Venerables, I have committed an offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. How should I proceed?” They reported the matter to the Blessed One. “In that case, monks, let the Sangha grant the monk Udāyī a five-day probation for that offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. And, monks, it should be granted thus:

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā añjaliṃ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbo. Tatiyampi yācitabbo. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

Then, monks, that monk Udāyī should approach the Sangha, arrange his upper robe over one shoulder, pay homage at the feet of the senior monks, kneel down, raise his joined palms, and say: ‘Venerables, I have committed one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. I ask the Sangha for five days’ probation for that one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days.’ He should make the request a second time. He should make the request a third time. A competent and capable monk should then inform the Sangha:

109. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

109.Venerables, may the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed an offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He asks the Sangha for five days’ probation for one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. If it is suitable for the Sangha, the Sangha may grant the monk Udāyī five days’ probation for one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. This is the motion.

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

Venerables, may the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed an offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He asks the Sangha for five days’ probation for one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Sangha grants the monk Udāyī five days’ probation for one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Any venerable one who approves of granting the monk Udāyī five days’ probation for one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days—should remain silent. Any one who disapproves should speak.

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

A second time I state this matter… A third time I state this matter…

‘‘Dinno saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāso. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

The Sangha has granted the monk Udāyī a five-day probation for one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Sangha approves, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.

Pārivāsikamūlāyapaṭikassanā

The drawing back to the root for a probationer.

110. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassatu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo –

110.While undergoing probation, he committed one deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. He informed the monks: "Friends, I committed one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. I requested the Sangha for a five-day probation for that one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Sangha granted me a five-day probation for that one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. While undergoing probation, I committed one deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. What should I do now?" They reported the matter to the Blessed One. "Well then, monks, let the Sangha draw back the monk Udāyī to the root for the intervening deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. And monks, he should be drawn back to the root thus:

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassanaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbā [yācitabbo (sī. evamuparipi)]. Tatiyampi yācitabbā [yācitabbo (sī. evamuparipi)]. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

"Monks, that monk Udāyī should approach the Sangha… and he should say thus: ‘Venerable sirs, I committed one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. I requested the Sangha for a five-day probation for that one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Sangha granted me a five-day probation for that one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. While undergoing probation, I committed one deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. Venerable sirs, I request the Sangha for a drawing back to the root on account of the intervening deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed.’ He should be requested a second time… He should be requested a third time. A competent and capable monk should inform the Sangha:

111. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikasseyya. Esā ñatti.

111."Venerable sirs, may the Sangha listen to me. This monk Udāyī has committed one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. He requested the Sangha for a five-day probation for that one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Sangha granted the monk Udāyī a five-day probation for that one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. While undergoing probation, he committed one deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. He requests the Sangha for a drawing back to the root for the intervening deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. If it seems appropriate to the Sangha, the Sangha should draw back the monk Udāyī to the root for the intervening deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. This is the announcement.

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassati. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

"Venerable sirs, may the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. He requested the Sangha for a five-day probation for that one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Sangha granted the monk Udāyī a five-day probation for that one deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. While undergoing probation, he committed another deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. He now requests the Sangha for a drawing back to the root for that one deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim. The Sangha draws back the monk Udāyī to the root for that one deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim. Let any venerable one who approves of the drawing back to the root of the monk Udāyī for that one deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim, remain silent. Let anyone who disapproves speak.

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

"A second time I state this matter… A third time I state this matter…"

‘‘Paṭikassito saṅghena udāyī bhikkhu antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā [mūlāya (syā.)]. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

The Sangha has drawn back the monk Udāyī to the root for that one deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim. The Sangha approves, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.

Mānattārahamūlāyapaṭikassanā

Relegation to the Beginning While Worthy of Mānatta

112. So parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassatu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo –

112.Having completed his probation and being worthy of mānatta, he committed another offense—a deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. He informed the monks: "Friends, I committed an offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. I requested the Sangha for a five-day probation for that deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Sangha granted me a five-day probation for that deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. While on probation, I committed another offense—a deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. I requested the Sangha to relegate me to the beginning for that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim. The Sangha relegated me to the beginning for that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim. Having completed my probation and being worthy of mānatta, I committed another offense—a deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. What should I do now?" They reported the matter to the Blessed One. "Well then, monks, let the Sangha relegate the monk Udāyī to the beginning for that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim. And this is how he should be relegated to the beginning—"

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbā. Tatiyampi yācitabbā. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

“Then, monks, the monk Udāyin should approach the Sangha and… should say this: ‘Venerable sirs, I committed one offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days… Having completed the period of probation and being worthy of mānatta, during that time I committed another offense—a deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. Therefore, I ask the Sangha to relegate me to the beginning for this one offense of deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim.’ He should make this request a second time and a third time. A competent and capable monk should inform the Sangha:

113. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… so parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikasseyya. Esā ñatti.

113.‘Venerable sirs, may the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days… Having completed his probation and being worthy of mānatta, he committed another offense—a deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. He now requests the Sangha to relegate him to the beginning for this one offense of deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim. If it is agreeable to the Sangha, let the Sangha relegate Udāyī to the beginning for this one offense of deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. This is the motion.

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… so parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassati. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

‘Venerable sirs, may the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyi has committed one offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days… Having completed his probation and being worthy of mānatta, he committed, in the interim, another offense—a deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. He now requests the Sangha to relegate him to the beginning for this one offense of deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim. The Sangha relegates Udāyi to the beginning for this one offense of deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. If any venerable one approves of relegating Udāyi to the beginning for this one offense of deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, let him remain silent. If any does not approve, let him speak.

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

‘For the second time I state this matter… For the third time I state this matter…

‘‘Paṭikassito saṅghena udāyī bhikkhu antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

‘The monk Udāyī has been relegated to the beginning by the Sangha for that one deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed, committed in the interim. The Sangha approves of it, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.’

Tikāpattimānattaṃ

Penance for Three Offenses

114. So parivutthaparivāso bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbaṃ –

114.Having completed the probationary period, he informed the monks: ‘Friends, I have committed an offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days… Having completed the probationary period, how should I proceed?’ They reported this matter to the Blessed One. ‘Well then, monks, let the Sangha impose a six-night penance on the monk Udāyī for three offenses. And it should be imposed like this—

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi…pe… sohaṃ, bhante, parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

Then, monks, that monk Udāyī should approach the Sangha and… should be addressed thus: ‘Venerable sirs, I committed one offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. I requested the Sangha for a five-day probationary period for that one deliberate offense of emission of semen concealed for five days. The Sangha granted me a five-day probationary period for that one deliberate offense of emission of semen concealed for five days… Now, venerable sirs, having completed the probationary period, I request the Sangha for a six-night penance for three offenses.’ A second time it should be requested. A third time it should be requested. A competent and capable monk should inform the Sangha:

115. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… so parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

115.Venerable sirs, may the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days… Having completed the probationary period, he now requests the Sangha for a six-night penance for three offenses. If the Sangha is ready, let the Sangha grant a six-night penance for three offenses to the monk Udāyī. This is the motion.

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… so parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

Venerable sirs, may the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days… He has completed his probationary period and now requests the Sangha for a six-night penance for three offenses. The Sangha grants a six-night penance for three offenses to the monk Udāyī. If it seems right to the venerable ones to grant a six-night penance for three offenses to the monk Udāyī, let them be silent. If it does not seem right to anyone, let them speak.

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

For the second time, I say this… For the third time, I say this…

‘‘Dinnaṃ saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

The Sangha has given the monk Udāyī a six-night penance for three offenses. The Sangha approves. Therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.

Mānattacārikamūlāyapaṭikassanā

The reversion to the beginning for one undergoing probation.

116. So mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo – tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbā. Tatiyampi yācitabbā. ‘‘Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

116.While undergoing probation, he committed an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed. He informed the monks: "Friends, I committed an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days… While undergoing probation, I committed an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed. What should I do now?" They reported the matter to the Blessed One. "Well then, monks, let the Sangha, having reverted the monk Udāyī to the beginning on account of an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed, give him a six-night probation. And monks, he should be reverted to the beginning thus: That monk Udāyī should approach the Sangha… and say: 'Venerable sirs, I committed an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days… While undergoing probation, I committed an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed. Venerable sirs, I ask the Sangha for reversion to the beginning on account of an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed.' He should ask a second time. He should ask a third time. A competent and capable monk should inform the Sangha:

117. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu…pe… mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikasseyya. Esā ñatti…pe… paṭikassito saṅghena udāyī bhikkhu antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmīti.

117."Venerable sirs, let the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyī ... asks for reversion to the beginning. If it is suitable for the Sangha, the Sangha may revert the monk Udāyī to the beginning for an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed. This is the motion ... The monk Udāyī has been reverted to the beginning by the Sangha for an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed. The Sangha approves, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it."

‘‘Evañca pana, bhikkhave, chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ – tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

"And monks, a six-night probation should be given thus: That monk Udāyī... should be addressed thus: 'Venerable sirs, I committed an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days... While undergoing probation, I committed an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed. I asked the Sangha for reversion to the beginning on account of an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed. The Sangha reverted me to the beginning on account of an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed. Venerable sirs, I ask the Sangha for a six-night probation on account of an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed.' He should be asked a second time. He should be asked a third time. A competent and capable monk should inform the Sangha:

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu…pe… chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti…pe… dinnaṃ saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

"Venerable sirs, may the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyī... asks for a six-night probation. If it is suitable for the Sangha, the Sangha should give the monk Udāyī a six-night probation on account of an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed. This is the motion... The Sangha has given the monk Udāyī a six-night probation on account of an intervening intentional emission of semen, unconcealed. The Sangha approves, therefore it is silent; thus I hold it."

Abbhānārahamūlāyapaṭikassanā

Drawing Back to the Root for One Worthy of Reinstatement.

118. So ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo…pe….

118.Having completed the probation, he was worthy of reinstatement, but in the meantime he committed one intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. He informed the monks: "Friends, I committed one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days... having completed the probation, I was worthy of reinstatement, but in the meantime I committed one intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. What should I do now?" They reported the matter to the Blessed One. "Well then, monks, let the Saṅgha, having drawn the monk Udāyī back to the root for one intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed, grant him six nights' probation. And, monks, he should be drawn back to the root like this..."

‘‘Evañca pana, bhikkhave, chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ…pe….

"And, monks, the six-night probation should be granted like this..."

‘‘Dinnaṃ saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

"The Saṅgha has granted the monk Udāyī six nights' probation for one intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha is agreeable, therefore it is silent; thus I hold it in mind."

Mūlāyapaṭikassitaabbhānaṃ

Reinstatement after being Drawn Back to the Root.

119. So ciṇṇamānatto bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbhetu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, abbhetabbo –

119.Having completed the probation, he announced to the monks: "Friends, I have committed an intentional offense involving the emission of semen, concealed for five days... having completed the probation... What should I do now?" They reported this matter to the Blessed One. "Well then, monks, let the Saṅgha reinstate the monk Udāyī. And, monks, he should be reinstated like this..."

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ, bhante, ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmī’’’ti.

"Then, mendicants, the monk Udāyī should approach the Saṅgha … and say this: ‘Venerable sirs, I committed one offense: a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. I requested the Saṅgha for a five-day probation for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Saṅgha granted me a five-day probation for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. While on probation, I committed another offense: a deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. I requested the Saṅgha to draw me back to the root for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha drew me back to the root for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. Having completed the probation, being eligible for probation, I committed another offense: a deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. I requested the Saṅgha to draw me back to the root for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha drew me back to the root for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. Having completed the probation, I requested the Saṅgha for a six-night probation for the three offenses. The Saṅgha granted me a six-night probation for the three offenses. While undertaking the probation, I committed another offense: a deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. I requested the Saṅgha to draw me back to the root for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha drew me back to the root for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. I requested the Saṅgha for a six-night probation for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha granted me a six-night probation for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. Having completed the probation, being eligible for reinstatement, I committed another offense: a deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. I requested the Saṅgha to draw me back to the root for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha drew me back to the root for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. I requested the Saṅgha for a six-night probation for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha granted me a six-night probation for that one offense, that deliberate emission of semen, unconcealed. Venerable sirs, having completed the probation, I ask the Saṅgha for reinstatement.’"

‘‘Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

"A second time it should be requested. A third time it should be requested. A competent and able bhikkhu should inform the Saṅgha:"

120. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. So parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. So parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheyya. Esā ñatti.

120."Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha listen to me. This monk Udāyī committed one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days. He requested the Saṅgha for a five-day probation for that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī a five-day probation for that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days. While on probation, he committed another intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. He requested the Saṅgha to draw him back to the root for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha drew the monk Udāyī back to the root for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. Having completed the probation, he became eligible for probation. Meanwhile, he committed another intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. He requested the Saṅgha to draw him back to the root for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha drew the monk Udāyī back to the root for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. Having completed the probation, he requested the Saṅgha for a six-night probation for the three offenses. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī a six-night probation for the three offenses. While undertaking the probation, he committed another intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. He requested the Saṅgha to draw him back to the root for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha drew the monk Udāyī back to the root for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. He then requested the Saṅgha for a six-night probation for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī a six-night probation for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. Having completed the probation, he became eligible for reinstatement. Meanwhile, he committed another intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. He requested the Saṅgha to draw him back to the root for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha drew the monk Udāyī back to the root for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. He then requested the Saṅgha for a six-night probation for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī a six-night probation for that additional intentional offense of emission of semen, unconcealed. Having completed the probation, he now requests the Saṅgha for reinstatement. If the Saṅgha is ready, may the Saṅgha reinstate the monk Udāyī. This is the motion."

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… so ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

"Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This monk Udāyī has committed an offense—intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days... He, having completed the probation, requests reinstatement by the Saṅgha. The Saṅgha reinstates the monk Udāyī. Whoever approves of the reinstatement of the monk Udāyī, let him be silent; whoever disapproves, let him speak."

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

"For the second time I state this matter... For the third time I state this matter..."

‘‘Abbhito saṅghena udāyī bhikkhu. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

The monk Udāyī has been reinstated by the Saṅgha. The Saṅgha approves, therefore it is silent. Thus I take it.

Pakkhappaṭicchannaparivāso

Probation for a Half-Month Concealment

121. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā udāyī ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpanno hoti sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo –

121.At that time the Venerable Udāyī had committed an offense: intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. He informed the monks, “Friends, I have committed an offense: intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. What should I do?” They reported this matter to the Blessed One. “Well then, monks, let the Saṅgha grant the monk Udāyī a half-month period of probation for that single offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. And, monks, it should be granted thus:

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbo. Tatiyampi yācitabbo. Byattena bhikkhuno paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

Then, monks, the monk Udāyī, having approached the Saṅgha… (and so on)… should be addressed thus: ‘Venerable sirs, I have committed an offense: intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. Venerable sirs, I request the Saṅgha for a half-month period of probation for that single offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month.’ He should make the request a second time; he should make the request a third time. A competent, able monk should inform the Saṅgha:

122. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

122.Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha listen to me. This monk Udāyī has committed a single offense: intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. He requests the Saṅgha for a half-month period of probation for that single offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. If it is appropriate for the Saṅgha, the Saṅgha should grant the monk Udāyī a half-month period of probation for that single offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. This is the motion.

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.
