Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha listen to me. This monk Udāyī has committed a single offense: intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. He requests the Saṅgha for a half-month period of probation for that single offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. The Saṅgha grants the monk Udāyī a half-month period of probation for that single offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. If the granting of a half-month period of probation to the monk Udāyī for that single offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month, is agreeable to any venerable one, he should be silent. If it is not agreeable, he should speak.

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

For a second time I state this matter… (and so on)… For a third time I state this matter… (and so on)…

‘‘Dinno saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāso. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

A half-month period of probation has been granted by the Saṅgha to the monk Udāyī for that single offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. The Saṅgha approves, therefore it is silent. Thus I take it.

Pakkhapārivāsikamūlāyapaṭikassanā

The Return to the Root for One Undergoing Half-Month Probation

123. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti! Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo –

123.While undergoing probation, he committed an intermediate intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He informed the monks: “Venerables, I committed an intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. I requested the Sangha for half a month’s probation for that intentional emission of semen concealed for half a month. The Sangha granted me half a month’s probation for that intentional emission of semen concealed for half a month. While undergoing probation, I committed an intermediate intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. What should I do now?” They reported the matter to the Blessed One. “In that case, monks, let the Sangha return the monk Udāyī to the root for the intermediate intentional emission of semen concealed for five days, and then give him combined probation for the former offense. And monks, he should be returned to the root like this:

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbā. Tatiyampi yācitabbā. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

“Monks, the monk Udāyī should approach the Sangha… and say this: ‘Venerables, I committed an intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. I requested the Sangha for half a month’s probation for that intentional emission of semen concealed for half a month. The Sangha granted me half a month’s probation for that intentional emission of semen concealed for half a month. While undergoing probation, I committed an intermediate intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Venerables, I request the Sangha for a return to the root for the intermediate intentional emission of semen concealed for five days.’ He should make the request a second time, and a third time. A competent and capable monk should then inform the Sangha:

124. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikasseyya. Esā ñatti.

124.“Venerable Sirs, let the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyī committed an intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. He requested the Sangha for half a month’s probation for that intentional emission of semen concealed for half a month. The Sangha granted the monk Udāyī half a month’s probation for that intentional emission of semen concealed for half a month. While undergoing probation, he committed an intermediate intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He now requests the Sangha for a return to the root for the intermediate intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. If it seems appropriate to the Sangha, the Sangha should return the monk Udāyī to the root for the intermediate intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. This is the motion.”

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassati. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

“Venerable Sirs, let the Sangha hear me. This monk Udāyī committed an intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. He requested the Sangha for half a month’s probation for that intentional emission of semen concealed for half a month. The Sangha granted the monk Udāyī half a month’s probation for that intentional emission of semen concealed for half a month. While undergoing probation, he committed an intermediate intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He requests the Sangha for a return to the root for the intermediate intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. The Sangha returns the monk Udāyī to the root for the intermediate intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. Whichever venerable approves of the Sangha’s returning the monk Udāyī to the root for the intermediate intentional emission of semen concealed for five days, let him be silent; whichever does not approve, let him speak.”

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

“For a second time I state this matter… For a third time I state this matter…”

‘‘Paṭikassito saṅghena udāyī bhikkhu antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

“The monk Udāyī has been returned to the root by the Sangha for the intermediate intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. The Sangha approves of it, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.”

Samodhānaparivāso

Combined Probation

125. ‘‘Evañca pana, bhikkhave, purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo – tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’’’ti.

125.“And thus, bhikkhus, combined probation for the earlier offense should be given. That bhikkhu Udāyī should approach the Saṅgha… and should say thus: ‘Venerable sirs, I committed one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight. I requested the Saṅgha for a fortnight’s probation for that offense, an intentional emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight. The Saṅgha granted me a fortnight’s probation for that offense, an intentional emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight. While on probation, I committed another offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. I requested the Saṅgha to send me back to the beginning for that offense, an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. The Saṅgha sent me back to the beginning for that offense, an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. Now, venerable sirs, I request the Saṅgha for combined probation for the earlier offense, on account of this offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim.’

‘‘Dutiyampi yācitabbo. Tatiyampi yācitabbo. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

He should be requested a second time. He should be requested a third time. A competent and able bhikkhu should inform the Saṅgha:

126. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

126.“Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha listen to me. This bhikkhu Udāyī committed one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight. He requested the Saṅgha for a fortnight’s probation for that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight. The Saṅgha granted bhikkhu Udāyī a fortnight’s probation for that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight. While on probation, he committed another offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He requested the Saṅgha to send him back to the beginning for that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. The Saṅgha sent bhikkhu Udāyī back to the beginning for that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. He requests the Saṅgha for combined probation for the earlier offense, on account of that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. If the Saṅgha is ready, the Saṅgha may grant bhikkhu Udāyī combined probation for the earlier offense, on account of that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. This is the motion.

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

“Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha listen to me. This bhikkhu Udāyī committed one offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight. He requested the Saṅgha for a fortnight’s probation for that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight. The Saṅgha granted bhikkhu Udāyī a fortnight’s probation for that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight. While on probation, he committed another offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He requested the Saṅgha to send him back to the beginning for that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. The Saṅgha sent bhikkhu Udāyī back to the beginning for that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. He requests the Saṅgha for combined probation for the earlier offense, on account of that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. The Saṅgha grants bhikkhu Udāyī combined probation for the earlier offense, on account of that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. If any venerable one approves of granting bhikkhu Udāyī combined probation for the earlier offense, on account of that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim, let him remain silent. If anyone disapproves, let him speak.”

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

For a second time I state this matter… For a third time I state this matter….

‘‘Dinno saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

“Combined probation for the earlier offense has been granted by the Saṅgha to bhikkhu Udāyī, on account of that one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, committed in the interim. The Saṅgha approves of it, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.”

Mānattārahamūlāyapaṭikassanādi

On Sending Back to the Beginning for One Deserving Penance, etc.

127. So parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo…pe….

127.A monk who had completed his probation and was deserving of penance meanwhile committed an intentional offense of semen emission, concealed for five days. He informed the monks: "Friends, I committed an intentional offense of semen emission, concealed for a fortnight... I had completed my probation and was deserving of penance when, meanwhile, I committed an intentional offense of semen emission, concealed for five days. What should I do?" They reported the matter to the Blessed One. [He replied:] "In that case, monks, the Sangha should send the monk Udāyi back to the beginning for that one intentional offense of semen emission, concealed for five days, and give him concurrent probation for the earlier offense. And this is how, monks, he should be sent back to the beginning..."

‘‘Evañca pana, bhikkhave, purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo…pe… deti…pe….

"And this is how, monks, concurrent probation for the earlier offense should be given... he gives... and so on."

‘‘Dinno saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

"The Sangha has given the monk Udāyi concurrent probation for the earlier offense, on account of the one intentional offense of semen emission, concealed for five days, committed meanwhile. The Sangha approves of it, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it."

Tikāpattimānattaṃ

Penance for Three Offenses

128. So parivutthaparivāso bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbaṃ –

128.The monk, having completed his probation, informed the monks: "Friends, I committed an intentional offense of semen emission, concealed for a fortnight... I have completed my probation. What should I do?" They reported the matter to the Blessed One. [He replied:] "In that case, monks, the Sangha should give the monk Udāyi six nights' penance for the three offenses. And this is how, monks, it should be given:"

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ, bhante, parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

"Then, monks, the monk Udāyin should approach the Sangha... and he should be addressed thus: 'Venerable sirs, I have committed an intentional offense of semen emission, concealed for a fortnight... Venerable sirs, having completed my probation, I request the Sangha for six nights' penance for three offenses.' He should make the request a second time. He should make the request a third time. A competent and capable monk should inform the Sangha:"

129. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… so parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

129."Venerable sirs, may the Sangha listen to me. This monk Udāyi has committed an intentional offense of semen emission, concealed for a fortnight... Having completed his probation, he requests the Sangha for six nights' penance for the three offenses. If it is agreeable to the Sangha, the Sangha should grant the monk Udāyi six nights' penance for the three offenses. This is the motion."

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… so parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

"Venerable sirs, may the Sangha listen to me. This monk Udāyi has committed an intentional offense of semen emission, concealed for a fortnight... Having completed his probation, he requests the Sangha for six nights' penance for the three offenses. The Sangha gives the monk Udāyi six nights' penance for the three offenses. Any venerable one who approves of the giving of six nights' penance for the three offenses to the monk Udāyi should remain silent; any who does not approve should speak."

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

"For the second time I say this... For the third time I say this..."

‘‘Dinnaṃ saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

"The Sangha has given the monk Udāyi six nights' penance for the three offenses. The Sangha approves of it, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it."

Mānattacārikamūlāyapaṭikassanādi

Reinstatement to the Origin for One Undergoing Probation, and So On

130. So mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ datvā chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo…pe….

130.While undergoing probation, he committed one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days. He informed the monks: "Friends, I committed one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight… While undergoing probation, I committed one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days. What should I do now?" They reported the matter to the Blessed One. "Well then, monks, the Sangha should reinstate the monk Udāyi to the origin on account of one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, and then grant him concurrent probation for the earlier offense, followed by six nights of probation. And this is how, monks, he should be reinstated to the origin…"

‘‘Evañca pana, bhikkhave, purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo…pe….

And this is how, monks, concurrent probation for the earlier offense should be given…

‘‘Evañca pana, bhikkhave, chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ…pe… deti…pe….

And this is how, monks, six nights of probation should be given…

‘‘Dinnaṃ saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

The Sangha has given the monk Udāyi six nights of probation for one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Sangha approves, therefore it is silent. Thus I remember it.

Abbhānārahamūlāyapaṭikassanādi

Reinstatement to the Origin for One Worthy of Rehabilitation, and So On

131. So ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ datvā chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo…pe….

131.Having completed probation and being worthy of rehabilitation, he committed one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days. He informed the monks: "Friends, I committed one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight… Having completed probation and being worthy of rehabilitation, I committed one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days. What should I do now?" They reported the matter to the Blessed One. "Well then, monks, the Sangha should reinstate the monk Udāyi to the origin on account of one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days, and then grant him concurrent probation for the earlier offense, followed by six nights of probation. And this is how, monks, he should be reinstated to the origin…"

‘‘Evañca pana, bhikkhave, purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo…pe….

And this is how, monks, concurrent probation for the earlier offense should be given…

‘‘Evañca pana, bhikkhave, chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ…pe… deti…pe….

And this is how, monks, six nights of probation should be given…

‘‘Dinnaṃ saṅghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

The Sangha has given the monk Udāyi six nights of probation for one intentional offense of emission of semen, concealed for five days. The Sangha approves, therefore it is silent. Thus I remember it.

Pakkhappaṭicchannaabbhānaṃ

Reinstatement for an Offense Concealed for a Fortnight

132. So ciṇṇamānatto bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbhetu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, abbhetabbo –

132.The monk, having completed the mānatta, informed the monks: "Friends, I have committed an offense—an intentional emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight... I have completed the mānatta. How should I proceed?" They reported the matter to the Blessed One. "In that case, monks, let the Sangha reinstate the monk Udāyi. And, monks, he should be reinstated as follows:—

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā, ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā, vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā, ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā, añjaliṃ paggahetvā, evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. Taṃ maṃ saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ, bhante, ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmī’’’ti.

"Then, monks, the monk Udāyi should approach the Sangha, arrange his upper robe over one shoulder, pay homage at the feet of the senior monks, sit in a squatting position, raise his joined palms, and should say thus: ‘Venerable sirs, I committed one offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for a fortnight. I requested the Sangha for a fortnight’s probation for that one offense, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for a fortnight. The Sangha granted me a fortnight’s probation for that one offense, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for a fortnight. While undergoing probation, I committed another offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. I requested the Sangha to send me back to the beginning for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. The Sangha sent me back to the beginning for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. I then requested the Sangha for combined probation for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days, along with the original offense. The Sangha granted me combined probation for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days, along with the original offense. Having completed the combined probation, I became eligible for mānatta. In the interim, I committed another offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. I requested the Sangha to send me back to the beginning for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. The Sangha sent me back to the beginning for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. I then requested the Sangha for combined probation for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days, along with the original offense. The Sangha granted me combined probation for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days, along with the original offense. Having completed the combined probation, I requested the Sangha for a six-night mānatta for the three offenses. The Sangha granted me a six-night mānatta for the three offenses. While undergoing mānatta, I committed another offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. I requested the Sangha to send me back to the beginning for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. The Sangha sent me back to the beginning for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. I then requested the Sangha for combined probation for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days, along with the original offense. The Sangha granted me combined probation for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days, along with the original offense. Having completed the combined probation, I requested the Sangha for a six-night mānatta for the offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. The Sangha granted me a six-night mānatta for the offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. Having completed mānatta, and being eligible for reinstatement, in the interim, I committed another offense—a deliberate emission of semen, concealed for five days. I requested the Sangha to send me back to the beginning for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. The Sangha sent me back to the beginning for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. I then requested the Sangha for combined probation for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days, along with the original offense. The Sangha granted me combined probation for that offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days, along with the original offense. Having completed the combined probation, I requested the Sangha for a six-night mānatta for the offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. The Sangha granted me a six-night mānatta for the offense committed in the interim, a deliberate emission of semen concealed for five days. Venerable sirs, having completed mānatta, I now request the Sangha for reinstatement.’

‘‘Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

"A second time it should be requested. A third time it should be requested. A competent and able bhikkhu should inform the Sangha:—

133. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ [so saṃghaṃ (ka.)] antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. So saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. So parivutthaparivāso saṅghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. Saṅgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. So ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheyya. Esā ñatti.

133."Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha listen to me. This monk Udāyī committed an offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month. He requested the Saṅgha for half a month’s probation for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for half a month. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī half a month’s probation for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for half a month. While undergoing probation, he committed another offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He requested the Saṅgha for relegation to the beginning for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. The Saṅgha relegated the monk Udāyī to the beginning for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. He then requested the Saṅgha for conjoined probation for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days with the previous offense. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī conjoined probation for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days with the previous offense. Having completed his probation, being eligible for mānatta, he committed another offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He requested the Saṅgha for relegation to the beginning for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. The Saṅgha relegated the monk Udāyī to the beginning for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. He then requested the Saṅgha for conjoined probation for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days with the previous offense. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī conjoined probation for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days with the previous offense. Having completed his probation, he requested the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for the three offenses. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī a six-night mānatta for the three offenses. While undergoing mānatta, he committed another offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He requested the Saṅgha for relegation to the beginning for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. The Saṅgha relegated the monk Udāyī to the beginning for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. He then requested the Saṅgha for conjoined probation for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days with the previous offense. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī conjoined probation for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days with the previous offense. Having completed his probation, he requested the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī a six-night mānatta for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. Having completed the mānatta, being eligible for rehabilitation, he committed another offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. He requested the Saṅgha for relegation to the beginning for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. The Saṅgha relegated the monk Udāyī to the beginning for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. He then requested the Saṅgha for conjoined probation for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days with the previous offense. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī conjoined probation for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days with the previous offense. Having completed his probation, he requested the Saṅgha for a six-night mānatta for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. The Saṅgha granted the monk Udāyī a six-night mānatta for that one offense of intentional emission of semen concealed for five days. Having completed the mānatta, he requests the Saṅgha for rehabilitation. If it is agreeable to the Saṅgha, the Saṅgha may rehabilitate the monk Udāyī. This is the motion."

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ…pe… so ciṇṇamānatto saṅghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. Saṅgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

"Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha listen to me. This monk Udāyī committed an offense: an intentional emission of semen, concealed for half a month... Having completed the mānatta, he requests the Saṅgha for rehabilitation. The Saṅgha rehabilitates the monk Udāyī. If the rehabilitation of the monk Udāyī is agreeable to any venerable one, let him be silent; if it is not agreeable, let him speak."

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

"For the second time I state this matter... For the third time I state this matter..."

‘‘Abbhito saṅghena udāyī bhikkhu. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

"The monk Udāyī has been rehabilitated by the Saṅgha. It is agreeable to the Saṅgha, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it."

Sukkavissaṭṭhi samattā.

"The section on emission of semen is concluded."

### 2. Parivāso ^2

> [!TIP]- Links to [[cv13-brahmali-pali#^2|Brahmali Version]] and BMC2

2.Probation

Agghasamodhānaparivāso

Probation by Valuation of Offenses

134. Tena kho pana samayena aññataro bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpanno hoti – ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti dvīhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti tīhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti catūhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti pañcāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti chāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti sattāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti aṭṭhāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti navāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ – ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā…pe… ekā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho tassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo –

134.At that time a certain bhikkhu had committed several Saṅghādisesa offenses: one offense concealed for one day, one offense concealed for two days, one offense concealed for three days, one offense concealed for four days, one offense concealed for five days, one offense concealed for six days, one offense concealed for seven days, one offense concealed for eight days, one offense concealed for nine days, and one offense concealed for ten days. He told the bhikkhus, “Friends, I have committed several Saṅghādisesa offenses: one offense concealed for one day … up to one offense concealed for ten days. What should I do?” They reported this matter to the Blessed One. “In that case, bhikkhus, let the Saṅgha grant that bhikkhu a combined probation for those offenses, reckoned by the offense concealed for ten days. And this is how it should be granted:

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ – ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā…pe… ekā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbo. Tatiyampi yācitabbo. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

That bhikkhu, bhikkhus, should approach the Saṅgha… and say: ‘Venerable Sirs, I have committed several Saṅghādisesa offenses: one offense concealed for one day… up to one offense concealed for ten days. I request the Saṅgha for a combined probation for those offenses, reckoned by the offense concealed for ten days.’ He should be asked a second time. He should be asked a third time. A competent and capable bhikkhu should inform the Saṅgha:

135. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji – ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā…pe… ekā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā. So saṅghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

135.Venerable Sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This bhikkhu named so-and-so has committed several Saṅghādisesa offenses: one offense concealed for one day… up to one offense concealed for ten days. He requests the Saṅgha for a combined probation for those offenses, reckoned by the offense concealed for ten days. If it is appropriate for the Saṅgha, the Saṅgha may grant a combined probation to this bhikkhu named so-and-so for those offenses, reckoned by the offense concealed for ten days. This is the motion.

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji – ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā…pe… ekā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā. So saṅghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. Saṅgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā; tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

Venerable Sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This bhikkhu named so-and-so has committed several Saṅghādisesa offenses: one offense concealed for one day… up to one offense concealed for ten days. He requests the Saṅgha for a combined probation for those offenses, reckoned by the offense concealed for ten days. The Saṅgha grants a combined probation to this bhikkhu named so-and-so for those offenses, reckoned by the offense concealed for ten days. Any venerable one who approves of granting a combined probation to this bhikkhu named so-and-so for those offenses, reckoned by the offense concealed for ten days, should remain silent. Any one who does not approve should speak.

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

For a second time, I state this matter… For a third time, I state this matter….

‘‘Dinno saṅghena itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāso. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

A combined probation has been granted by the Saṅgha to this bhikkhu named so-and-so for those offenses, reckoned by the offense concealed for ten days. The Saṅgha approves of it, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.

Sabbacirappaṭicchannaagghasamodhānaṃ

Combined Probation Reckoned by All Longest-Concealed Offenses

136. Tena kho pana samayena aññataro bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpanno hoti – ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā, dve āpattiyo dvīhappaṭicchannāyo [dvīhappaṭicchannā (ka. evaṃ yāvadasāhappaṭicchannā)], tisso āpattiyo tīhappaṭicchannāyo, catasso āpattiyo catūhappaṭicchannāyo, pañca āpattiyo pañcāhappaṭicchannāyo, cha āpattiyo chāhappaṭicchannāyo, satta āpattiyo sattāhappaṭicchannāyo, aṭṭha āpattiyo aṭṭhāhappaṭicchannāyo, nava āpattiyo navāhappaṭicchannāyo, dasa āpattiyo dasāhappaṭicchannāyo. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ, ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā…pe… dasa āpattiyo dasāhappaṭicchannāyo. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho tassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo –

136.At that time a certain bhikkhu had committed several Saṅghādisesa offenses: one offense concealed for one day, two offenses concealed for two days, three offenses concealed for three days, four offenses concealed for four days, five offenses concealed for five days, six offenses concealed for six days, seven offenses concealed for seven days, eight offenses concealed for eight days, nine offenses concealed for nine days, and ten offenses concealed for ten days. He told the bhikkhus: “Friends, I have committed several Saṅghādisesa offenses: one offense concealed for one day… up to ten offenses concealed for ten days. What should I do?” They reported this matter to the Blessed One. “In that case, bhikkhus, let the Saṅgha grant that bhikkhu a combined probation for those offenses, reckoned by the offenses that were concealed for the longest time. And this is how it should be granted:

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā…pe… evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ, ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā…pe… dasa āpattiyo dasāhappaṭicchannāyo. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. Dutiyampi yācitabbo. Tatiyampi yācitabbo. ‘‘Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

That bhikkhu, bhikkhus, should approach the Saṅgha… and say: ‘Venerable Sirs, I have committed several Saṅghādisesa offenses: one offense concealed for one day… up to ten offenses concealed for ten days. So, Venerable Sirs, I request the Saṅgha for a combined probation for those offenses, reckoned by the offenses that were concealed for the longest time.’ He should be asked a second time. He should be asked a third time. A competent and capable bhikkhu should inform the Saṅgha:

137. Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji, ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā…pe… dasa āpattiyo dasāhappaṭicchannāyo. So saṅghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ saṅgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

137.Venerable Sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This bhikkhu named so-and-so has committed several Saṅghādisesa offenses: one offense concealed for one day… up to ten offenses concealed for ten days. He requests the Saṅgha for a combined probation for those offenses, reckoned by the offenses that were concealed for the longest time. If it is appropriate for the Saṅgha, the Saṅgha may grant a combined probation to this bhikkhu named so-and-so for those offenses, reckoned by the offenses that were concealed for the longest time. This is the motion.

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji – ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā…pe… dasa āpattiyo dasāhappaṭicchannāyo. So saṅghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. Saṅgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

Venerable Sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This bhikkhu named so-and-so has committed several Saṅghādisesa offenses: one offense concealed for one day… up to ten offenses concealed for ten days. He requests the Saṅgha for a combined probation for those offenses, reckoned by the offenses that were concealed for the longest time. The Saṅgha grants a combined probation to this bhikkhu named so-and-so for those offenses, reckoned by the offenses that were concealed for the longest time. Any venerable one who approves of granting a combined probation to this bhikkhu named so-and-so for those offenses, reckoned by the offenses that were concealed for the longest time, should remain silent. Any one who does not approve should speak.

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

For a second time, I state this matter… For a third time, I state this matter….

‘‘Dinno saṅghena itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāso. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti.

A combined probation has been granted by the Saṅgha to this bhikkhu named so-and-so for those offenses, reckoned by the offenses that were concealed for the longest time. The Saṅgha approves of it, therefore it is silent. Thus I hold it.

Dvemāsaparivāso

Two-month probation.

138. Tena kho pana samayena aññataro bhikkhu dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpanno hoti dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa etadahosi – ‘‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’’nti. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. Tassa saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami – ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi – ‘‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyanti. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’’nti.

138.At that time, a certain bhikkhu had incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. It occurred to him: “I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months?” So he asked the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted him a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. While he was undergoing probation, a sense of shame overcame him: “I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. It occurred to me: ‘I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months?’ So I asked the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. While I was undergoing probation, a sense of shame overcame me. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for the other offense as well, concealed for two months?”

So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi – ‘‘ahaṃ, āvuso, dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami – ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami – yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyanti. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabba’’nti? Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. ‘‘Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṅgho tassa bhikkhuno itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ detu. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo –

That bhikkhu informed the bhikkhus: “Friends, I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. It occurred to me: ‘I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one of these offenses concealed for two months?’ So I asked the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one of the offenses concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me a two-month probation for one of the offenses concealed for two months. While I was observing the probation, a sense of shame arose in me: ‘I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. It occurred to me: “I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one of these offenses concealed for two months?” So I asked the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one of the offenses concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me a two-month probation for one of the offenses concealed for two months. While I was observing the probation, a sense of shame arose in me. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for the other offense as well, concealed for two months?’ How should I proceed?” They reported the matter to the Blessed One. “Well then, bhikkhus, let the Saṅgha grant that bhikkhu a two-month probation for the other offense concealed for two months. And this is how it should be given:

‘‘Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā saṅghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā, ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā, vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā, ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā, añjaliṃ paggahetvā, evamassa vacanīyo – ‘ahaṃ, bhante, dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi – ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami – ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami – yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyanti. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācāmīti.

“Then, bhikkhus, that bhikkhu should approach the Saṅgha, arrange his upper robe over one shoulder, pay homage at the feet of the senior bhikkhus, sit in a squatting position, raise his joined hands, and say: ‘Venerable sirs, I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. It occurred to me: “I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months?” So I asked the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. While I was undergoing probation, a sense of shame overcame me: “I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. It occurred to me: ‘I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months?’ So I asked the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. While I was undergoing probation, a sense of shame overcame me. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for the other offense as well, concealed for two months?’ Therefore, venerable sirs, I ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for the other offense concealed for two months.’ ”

‘‘Dutiyampi yācitabbo. Tatiyampi yācitabbo. ‘‘Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṅgho ñāpetabbo –

“He should be requested a second time. He should be requested a third time. A competent and capable bhikkhu should inform the Saṅgha:

139. ‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa etadahosi – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. Tassa saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami – ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyanti. So saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṃ, saṅgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. Esā ñatti.

139.“Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This bhikkhu, named so-and-so, has incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. It occurred to him: ‘I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months?’ So he asked the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted him a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. While he was undergoing probation, a sense of shame overcame him: ‘I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. It occurred to me: “I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months?” So I asked the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. While I was undergoing probation, a sense of shame overcame me. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for the other offense as well, concealed for two months?” He asks the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for the other offense concealed for two months. If it seems appropriate to the Saṅgha, the Saṅgha may grant the bhikkhu, named so-and-so, a two-month probation for the other offense concealed for two months. This is the motion.”

‘‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṅgho. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa etadahosi – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. Tassa saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami – ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyanti. So saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Saṅgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. Yassāyasmato khamati itthannāmassa bhikkhuno itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya.

“Venerable sirs, may the Saṅgha hear me. This bhikkhu, named so-and-so, has incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. It occurred to him: ‘I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months?’ So he asked the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted him a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. While he was undergoing probation, a sense of shame overcame him: ‘I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. It occurred to me: “I have incurred two Saṅghādisesa offenses, concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months?” So I asked the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me a two-month probation for one offense concealed for two months. While I was undergoing probation, a sense of shame overcame me. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for the other offense as well, concealed for two months?” He asks the Saṅgha for a two-month probation for the other offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha grants the bhikkhu, named so-and-so, a two-month probation for the other offense concealed for two months. If the venerable ones approve of granting the bhikkhu, named so-and-so, a two-month probation for the other offense concealed for two months, let them remain silent. If anyone disapproves, let them speak.”

‘‘Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe… tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi…pe….

“For the second time, I say this… For the third time, I say this….”

‘‘Dinno saṅghena itthannāmassa bhikkhuno itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāso. Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’’ti. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā tadupādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā.

“The Saṅgha has granted the bhikkhu named so-and-so two months’ probation for another offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha approves, therefore it is silent; thus I hold it.” Therefore, bhikkhus, that bhikkhu should undergo probation for two months beginning from that point.

Dve māsā parivasitabbavidhi

The Procedure for Two Months’ Probation

140. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa evaṃ hoti – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. So saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Tassa saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi – ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyanti. So saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Tassa saṅgho itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā tadupādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā.

140.“Here, bhikkhus, a bhikkhu commits two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. It occurs to him thus: ‘I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for one offense concealed for two months?’ He asks the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for one offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha grants him two months’ probation for one offense concealed for two months. While he is undergoing probation, a sense of shame comes upon him: ‘I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. It occurred to me thus: “I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for one offense concealed for two months?” So I asked the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for one offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me two months’ probation for one offense concealed for two months. While I am undergoing probation, a sense of shame has come upon me. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months as well?’ He asks the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha grants him two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months. Therefore, bhikkhus, that bhikkhu should undergo probation for two months beginning from that point.

141. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekaṃ āpattiṃ jānāti, ekaṃ āpattiṃ na jānāti. So saṅghaṃ yaṃ āpattiṃ jānāti tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Tassa saṅgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. So parivasanto itarampi āpattiṃ jānāti. Tassa evaṃ hoti – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekaṃ āpattiṃ jāniṃ, ekaṃ āpattiṃ na jāniṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ yaṃ āpattiṃ jāniṃ tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto itarampi āpattiṃ jānāmi. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. So saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Tassa saṅgho itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā tadupādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā.

141.“Here, bhikkhus, a bhikkhu commits two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. He knows one offense, but does not know the other. He asks the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the offense he knows, which was concealed for two months. The Saṅgha grants him two months’ probation for that offense concealed for two months. While undergoing probation, he comes to know the other offense as well. It occurs to him thus: ‘I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. I knew one offense, but did not know the other. So I asked the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the offense I knew, which was concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me two months’ probation for that offense concealed for two months. While undergoing probation, I have come to know the other offense as well. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months as well?’ He asks the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha grants him two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months. Therefore, bhikkhus, that bhikkhu should undergo probation for two months beginning from that point.”

142. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekaṃ āpattiṃ sarati, ekaṃ āpattiṃ nassarati. So saṅghaṃ yaṃ āpattiṃ sarati tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Tassa saṅgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. So parivasanto itarampi āpattiṃ sarati. Tassa evaṃ hoti – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekaṃ āpattiṃ sariṃ, ekaṃ āpattiṃ nassariṃ. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ yaṃ āpattiṃ sariṃ, tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto itarampi āpattiṃ sarāmi. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. So saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Tassa saṅgho itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā tadupādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā.

142.“Here, bhikkhus, a bhikkhu commits two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. He remembers one offense, but does not remember the other. He asks the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the offense he remembers, which was concealed for two months. The Saṅgha grants him two months’ probation for that offense concealed for two months. While undergoing probation, he remembers the other offense as well. It occurs to him thus: ‘I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. I remembered one, but did not remember the other. So I asked the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the offense I remembered, which was concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me two months’ probation for that offense concealed for two months. While undergoing probation, I have remembered the other offense as well. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months as well?’ He asks the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha grants him two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months. Therefore, bhikkhus, that bhikkhu should undergo probation for two months beginning from that point.

143. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekāya āpattiyā nibbematiko, ekāya āpattiyā vematiko. So saṅghaṃ yāya āpattiyā nibbematiko tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Tassa saṅgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. So parivasanto itarissāpi āpattiyā nibbematiko hoti. Tassa evaṃ hoti – ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekāya āpattiyā nibbematiko, ekāya āpattiyā vematiko. Sohaṃ saṅghaṃ yāya āpattiyā nibbematiko tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṅgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto itarissāpi āpattiyā nibbematiko. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyya’nti. So saṅghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Tassa saṅgho itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā tadupādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā.

143.“Here, bhikkhus, a bhikkhu commits two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. He is certain about one offense, but uncertain about the other. He asks the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the offense he is certain about, which was concealed for two months. The Saṅgha grants him two months’ probation for that offense concealed for two months. While undergoing probation, he becomes certain about the other offense as well. It occurs to him thus: ‘I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. I was certain about one, but uncertain about the other. So I asked the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the offense I was certain about, which was concealed for two months. The Saṅgha granted me two months’ probation for that offense concealed for two months. While undergoing probation, I have become certain about the other offense as well. What if I were to ask the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months as well?’ He asks the Saṅgha for two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months. The Saṅgha grants him two months’ probation for the other offense concealed for two months. Therefore, bhikkhus, that bhikkhu should undergo probation for two months beginning from that point.

144. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekā āpatti jānappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti ajānappaṭicchannā. So saṅghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Tassa saṅgho tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. Tassa parivasantassa añño bhikkhu āgacchati bahussuto āgatāgamo dhammadharo vinayadharo mātikādharo paṇḍito viyatto medhāvī lajjī kukkuccako sikkhākāmo.
