> "VIN-CV13.4" file:bmc2 -queryblock
> ```


4.The Thirty-Six

165. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu parivasanto antarā sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati parimāṇā [parimāṇāyo (sī. syā.)] appaṭicchannāyo. So bhikkhu mūlāya paṭikassitabbo.

165.Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu undergoing probation commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses in the interim that are quantifiable and unconcealed, that bhikkhu should be drawn back to the root.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu parivasanto antarā sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati parimāṇā paṭicchannāyo. So bhikkhu mūlāya paṭikassitabbo. Yathāpaṭicchannānañcassa āpattīnaṃ purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu undergoing probation commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses in the interim that are quantifiable and concealed, that bhikkhu should be drawn back to the root. And for those offenses as they were concealed, a probation of concurrence with the first offense should be given.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu parivasanto antarā sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati parimāṇā paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi. So bhikkhu mūlāya paṭikassitabbo. Yathāpaṭicchannānañcassa āpattīnaṃ purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu undergoing probation commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses in the interim that are quantifiable, both concealed and unconcealed, that bhikkhu should be drawn back to the root. And for those offenses as they were concealed, a probation of concurrence with the first offense should be given.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu parivasanto antarā sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati aparimāṇā [aparimāṇāyo (sī. syā.)] appaṭicchannāyo…pe… aparimāṇā paṭicchannāyo…pe… aparimāṇā paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi…pe… parimāṇāyopi aparimāṇāyopi appaṭicchannāyo…pe… parimāṇāyopi aparimāṇāyopi paṭicchannāyo…pe… parimāṇāyopi aparimāṇāyopi paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi. So bhikkhu mūlāya paṭikassitabbo. Yathāpaṭicchannānañcassa āpattīnaṃ purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu undergoing probation commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses in the interim that are unquantifiable and unconcealed… unquantifiable and concealed… unquantifiable, both concealed and unconcealed… both quantifiable and unquantifiable, unconcealed… both quantifiable and unquantifiable, concealed… both quantifiable and unquantifiable, both concealed and unconcealed, that bhikkhu should be drawn back to the root. And for those offenses as they were concealed, a probation of concurrence with the first offense should be given.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu mānattāraho…pe… mānattaṃ caranto…pe… (yathāparivāsaṃ tathā vitthāretabbaṃ) abbhānāraho antarā sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati parimāṇā appaṭicchannāyo…pe… parimāṇā paṭicchannāyo…pe… parimāṇā paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi…pe… aparimāṇā appaṭicchannāyo…pe… aparimāṇā paṭicchannāyo…pe… aparimāṇā paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi…pe… parimāṇāyopi aparimāṇāyopi appaṭicchannāyo…pe… parimāṇāyopi aparimāṇāyopi paṭicchannāyo…pe… parimāṇāyopi aparimāṇāyopi paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi. So bhikkhu mūlāya paṭikassitabbo. Yathāpaṭicchannānañcassa āpattīnaṃ purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu deserving mānatta… or undergoing mānatta… or deserving rehabilitation commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses in the interim that are quantifiable and unconcealed… quantifiable and concealed… quantifiable, both concealed and unconcealed… unquantifiable and unconcealed… unquantifiable and concealed… unquantifiable, both concealed and unconcealed… both quantifiable and unquantifiable, unconcealed… both quantifiable and unquantifiable, concealed… both quantifiable and unquantifiable, both concealed and unconcealed, that bhikkhu should be drawn back to the root. And for those offenses as they were concealed, a probation of concurrence with the first offense should be given.

Chattiṃsakaṃ samattaṃ.

The Thirty-sixth [Section] is completed.

### 5. Mānattasatakaṃ ^5

> [!TIP]- Links to [[cv13-brahmali-pali#^5|Brahmali Version]] and BMC2 
> [[bmc2#^ch19|BMC Chapter 19]] and the following cites:
>  
> ```query
> "VIN-CV13.5" file:bmc2 -queryblock
> ```


5.The Hundred on Mānatta

166. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjitvā appaṭicchādetvā vibbhamati. So puna [so ce puna (ka.)] upasampanno tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

166.Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses without concealing them and then disrobes, and having been reordained, he does not conceal those offenses, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, should be given mānatta.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjitvā appaṭicchādetvā vibbhamati. So puna upasampanno tā āpattiyo chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno pacchimasmiṃ āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses without concealing them and then disrobes, and having been reordained, he conceals those offenses, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for the later aggregate of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjitvā paṭicchādetvā vibbhamati. So puna upasampanno tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiṃ āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses, having concealed them, and then disrobes, and having been reordained, he does not conceal those offenses, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for the earlier aggregate of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjitvā paṭicchādetvā vibbhamati. So puna upasampanno tā āpattiyo chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses, having concealed them, and then disrobes, and having been reordained, he conceals those offenses, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

167. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Tassa honti āpattiyo paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nacchādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nacchādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiṃ āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

167.Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses, some of which are concealed and some unconcealed, and having disrobed and been reordained, he does not conceal those offenses he previously concealed, and he does not conceal those offenses he previously did not conceal, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for the earlier aggregate of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Tassa honti āpattiyo paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nacchādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses, some of which are concealed and some unconcealed, and having disrobed and been reordained, he does not conceal those offenses he previously concealed, and he conceals those offenses he previously did not conceal, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Tassa honti āpattiyo paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā chādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nacchādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses, some of which are concealed and some unconcealed, and having disrobed and been reordained, he conceals those offenses he previously concealed, and he does not conceal those offenses he previously did not conceal, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Tassa honti āpattiyo paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā chādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses, some of which are concealed and some unconcealed, and having disrobed and been reordained, he conceals those offenses he previously concealed, and he does not conceal those offenses he previously did not conceal, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

168. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccā āpattiyo jānāti, ekaccā āpattiyo na jānāti. Yā āpattiyo jānāti tā āpattiyo chādeti. Yā āpattiyo na jānāti tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe jānitvā chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā jānitvā nacchādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe ajānitvā nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā jānitvā nacchādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiṃ āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

168.Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses, knowing some and not knowing others, and he conceals the offenses he knows and does not conceal the offenses he does not know; and having disrobed and been reordained, he later knows and does not conceal those offenses he previously knew and concealed, and he later knows and does not conceal those offenses he previously did not know and did not conceal, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for the earlier aggregate of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccā āpattiyo jānāti, ekaccā āpattiyo na jānāti. Yā āpattiyo jānāti tā āpattiyo chādeti. Yā āpattiyo na jānāti tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe jānitvā chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā jānitvā nacchādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe ajānitvā nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā jānitvā chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses, knowing some and not knowing others, and he conceals the offenses he knows and does not conceal the offenses he does not know; and having disrobed and been reordained, he later knows and does not conceal those offenses he previously knew and concealed, and he later knows and conceals those offenses he previously did not know and did not conceal, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccā āpattiyo jānāti, ekaccā āpattiyo na jānāti. Yā āpattiyo jānāti tā āpattiyo chādeti. Yā āpattiyo na jānāti tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe jānitvā chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā jānitvā chādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe ajānitvā nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā jānitvā nacchādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses, knowing some and not knowing others, and he conceals the offenses he knows and does not conceal the offenses he does not know; and having disrobed and been reordained, he later knows and conceals those offenses he previously knew and concealed, and he later knows and does not conceal those offenses he previously did not know and did not conceal, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccā āpattiyo jānāti, ekaccā āpattiyo na jānāti. Yā āpattiyo jānāti tā āpattiyo chādeti; yā āpattiyo na jānāti tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe jānitvā chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā jānitvā chādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe ajānitvā nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā jānitvā chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

Here, bhikkhus, if a bhikkhu commits many Saṅghādisesa offenses, knowing some and not knowing others, and he conceals the offenses he knows and does not conceal the offenses he does not know; and having disrobed and been reordained, he later knows and conceals those offenses he previously knew and concealed, and he later knows and does not conceal those offenses he previously did not know and did not conceal, that bhikkhu, bhikkhus, having given probation for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, should be given mānatta.

169. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccā āpattiyo sarati, ekaccā āpattiyo nassarati. Yā āpattiyo sarati tā āpattiyo chādeti; yā āpattiyo nassarati tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe saritvā chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā saritvā nacchādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe assaritvā nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā saritvā nacchādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiṃ āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

169."Here, monks, a monk commits several Saṅghādisesa offenses. He remembers some offenses, but does not remember others. Those offenses he remembers, he conceals; those he does not remember, he does not conceal. Having lapsed and been reordained, those offenses he previously remembered and concealed, he later remembers and does not conceal; those he previously did not remember and did not conceal, he later remembers and does not conceal. For that monk, monks, probation should be given for the earlier aggregate of offenses as they were concealed, and then mānatta should be given."

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccā āpattiyo sarati, ekaccā āpattiyo nassarati. Yā āpattiyo sarati tā āpattiyo chādeti; yā āpattiyo nassarati tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe saritvā chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā saritvā nacchādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe assaritvā nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā saritvā chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

"Here, monks, a monk commits several Saṅghādisesa offenses. He remembers some offenses, but does not remember others. Those offenses he remembers, he conceals; those he does not remember, he does not conceal. Having lapsed and been reordained, those offenses he previously remembered and concealed, he later remembers and does not conceal; those he previously did not remember and did not conceal, he later remembers and conceals. For that monk, monks, probation should be given for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, and then mānatta should be given."

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccā āpattiyo sarati, ekaccā āpattiyo nassarati. Yā āpattiyo sarati tā āpattiyo chādeti; yā āpattiyo nassarati tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe saritvā chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā saritvā chādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe assaritvā nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā saritvā nacchādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

"Here, monks, a monk commits several Saṅghādisesa offenses. He remembers some offenses, but does not remember others. Those offenses he remembers, he conceals; those he does not remember, he does not conceal. Having lapsed and been reordained, those offenses he previously remembered and concealed, he later remembers and conceals; those he previously did not remember and did not conceal, he later remembers and does not conceal. For that monk, monks, probation should be given for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, and then mānatta should be given."

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccā āpattiyo sarati, ekaccā āpattiyo nassarati. Yā āpattiyo sarati tā āpattiyo chādeti; yā āpattiyo nassarati tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe saritvā chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā saritvā chādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe assaritvā nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā saritvā chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

"Here, monks, a monk commits several Saṅghādisesa offenses. He remembers some offenses, but does not remember others. Those offenses he remembers, he conceals; those he does not remember, he does not conceal. Having lapsed and been reordained, those offenses he previously remembered and concealed, he later remembers and conceals; those he previously did not remember and did not conceal, he later remembers and conceals. For that monk, monks, probation should be given for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, and then mānatta should be given."

170. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccāsu āpattīsu nibbematiko, ekaccāsu āpattīsu vematiko. Yāsu āpattīsu nibbematiko tā āpattiyo chādeti; yāsu āpattīsu vematiko tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe nibbematiko chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko nacchādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe vematiko nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko nacchādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiṃ āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

170."Here, monks, a monk commits several Saṅghādisesa offenses. Regarding some offenses, he is certain; regarding others, he is uncertain. Those offenses he is certain about, he conceals; those he is uncertain about, he does not conceal. Having lapsed and been reordained, those offenses he was previously certain about and concealed, he later becomes certain about and does not conceal; those he was previously uncertain about and did not conceal, he later becomes certain about and does not conceal. For that monk, monks, probation should be given for the earlier aggregate of offenses as they were concealed, and then mānatta should be given."

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccāsu āpattīsu nibbematiko, ekaccāsu āpattīsu vematiko. Yāsu āpattīsu nibbematiko tā āpattiyo chādeti; yāsu āpattīsu vematiko tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe nibbematiko chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko nacchādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe vematiko nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

"Here, monks, a monk commits several Saṅghādisesa offenses. Regarding some offenses, he is certain; regarding others, he is uncertain. Those offenses he is certain about, he conceals; those he is uncertain about, he does not conceal. Having lapsed and been reordained, those offenses he was previously certain about and concealed, he later becomes certain about and does not conceal; those he was previously uncertain about and did not conceal, he later becomes certain about and conceals. For that monk, monks, probation should be given for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, and then mānatta should be given."

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccāsu āpattīsu nibbematiko, ekaccāsu āpattīsu vematiko. Yāsu āpattīsu nibbematiko tā āpattiyo chādeti; yāsu āpattīsu vematiko tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe nibbematiko chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko chādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe vematiko nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko nacchādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

"Here, monks, a monk commits several Saṅghādisesa offenses. Regarding some offenses, he is certain; regarding others, he is uncertain. Those offenses he is certain about, he conceals; those he is uncertain about, he does not conceal. Having lapsed and been reordained, those offenses he was previously certain about and concealed, he later becomes certain about and conceals; those he was previously uncertain about and did not conceal, he later becomes certain about and does not conceal. For that monk, monks, probation should be given for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, and then mānatta should be given."

‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati. Ekaccāsu āpattīsu nibbematiko, ekaccāsu āpattīsu vematiko. Yāsu āpattīsu nibbematiko tā āpattiyo chādeti; yāsu āpattīsu vematiko tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vibbhamitvā puna upasampanno yā āpattiyo pubbe nibbematiko chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko chādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe vematiko nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

"Here, monks, a monk commits several Saṅghādisesa offenses. Regarding some offenses, he is certain; regarding others, he is uncertain. Those offenses he is certain about, he conceals; those he is uncertain about, he does not conceal. Having lapsed and been reordained, those offenses he was previously certain about and concealed, he later becomes certain about and conceals; those he was previously uncertain about and did not conceal, he later becomes certain about and conceals. For that monk, monks, probation should be given for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, and then mānatta should be given."

171. ‘‘Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sambahulā saṅghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjitvā appaṭicchādetvā sāmaṇero hoti…pe… ummattako hoti…pe… khittacitto hoti…pe… (yathā heṭṭhā tathā vitthāretabbaṃ) vedanāṭṭo hoti…pe… tassa honti āpattiyo paṭicchannāyopi appaṭicchannāyopi…pe… ekaccā āpattiyo jānāti, ekaccā āpattiyo na jānāti…pe… ekaccā āpattiyo sarati, ekaccā āpattiyo nassarati…pe… ekaccāsu āpattīsu nibbematiko, ekaccāsu āpattīsu vematiko. Yāsu āpattīsu nibbematiko tā āpattiyo chādeti; yāsu āpattīsu vematiko tā āpattiyo nacchādeti. So vedanāṭṭo hoti. So puna avedanāṭṭo hutvā yā āpattiyo pubbe nibbematiko chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko nacchādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe vematiko nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko nacchādeti…pe… yā āpattiyo pubbe nibbematiko chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko nacchādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe vematiko nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko chādeti…pe… yā āpattiyo pubbe nibbematiko chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko chādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe vematiko nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko nacchādeti…pe… yā āpattiyo pubbe nibbematiko chādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko chādeti; yā āpattiyo pubbe vematiko nacchādesi tā āpattiyo pacchā nibbematiko chādeti. Tassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno purimasmiñca pacchimasmiñca āpattikkhandhe yathāpaṭicchanne parivāsaṃ datvā mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ.

171."Here, monks, a monk commits several Saṅghādisesa offenses without concealing them and becomes a novice monk... becomes insane... becomes mentally deranged... (as above, so in detail) becomes afflicted by pain... For him, there are offenses both concealed and unconcealed... He knows some offenses, does not know some offenses... remembers some offenses, does not remember some offenses... is certain about some offenses, uncertain about some offenses. Those offenses he is certain about, he conceals; those he is uncertain about, he does not conceal. He is afflicted by pain. Then, becoming unafflicted by pain again, those offenses he was previously certain about and concealed, he later becomes certain about and does not conceal; those he was previously uncertain about and did not conceal, he later becomes certain about and does not conceal... those offenses he was previously certain about and concealed, he later becomes certain about and does not conceal; those he was previously uncertain about and did not conceal, he later becomes certain about and conceals... those offenses he was previously certain about and concealed, he later becomes certain about and conceals; those he was previously uncertain about and did not conceal, he later becomes certain about and does not conceal... those offenses he was previously certain about and concealed, he later becomes certain about and conceals; those he was previously uncertain about and did not conceal, he later becomes certain about and conceals. For that monk, monks, probation should be given for both the earlier and later aggregates of offenses as they were concealed, and then mānatta should be given."

Mānattasataṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

The hundredfold mānatta is concluded.

### 6. Samūlāyasamodhānaparivāsacatussataṃ ^6

> [!TIP]- Links to [[cv13-brahmali-pali#^6|Brahmali Version]] and BMC2 
> [[bmc2#^ch19|BMC Chapter 19]] and the following cites:
